Â  Â  Â  Â  function updateProgressBar() {

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const questionCount = quizSteps.filter(s => s.type === 'question').length;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const questionsAnswered = studentData.scores.filter(s => s !== undefined).length;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const progress = (questionsAnswered / questionCount) * 100;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const bar = document.getElementById('progress-bar');

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  bar.style.width = `${progress}%`;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  bar.innerText = `${Math.round(progress)}%`;

Â  Â  Â  Â  }

Â  Â  Â  Â  function updateWordCounter() {

Â Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const answer = document.getElementById('student-answer').value;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const wordCount = answer.trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).length;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const counter = document.getElementById('word-counter');

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  counter.innerText = `${wordCount}/50 à¸„à¸³`;

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  counter.style.color = wordCount > 50 ? 'red' : '#888';

Â  Â  Â  Â  }


Â  Â  Â  Â  document.getElementById('student-answer').addEventListener('input', updateWordCounter);

Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  const questionCount = quizSteps.filter(s => s.type === 'question').length;
